and what we're finding is that a lot of it is in the marine environment .	我們發現 , 大部份是在海洋環境中 。
i then , in the last few years , learned about the pacific garbage patch and the gyre .	然後 , 在過去幾年 , 我學到太平洋垃圾貼片和gyre 。
and my initial reaction and i think this is a lot of people's first reaction to learning about it is , " oh my god !	我最初的反應和我認為這是很多人第一次對它的反應: 「 天啊 !
we've got to go out there and clean this thing up . "	我們得要走出去 , 把這東西清理乾淨 。 」
so i actually developed a proposal to go out with a cargo ship and two decommissioned fishing trawlers , a crane , a chipping machine and a coldmolding machine .	因此 , 我提出了一個提案 , 要帶著一艘貨船出去 , 和兩艘退化的捕魚拖網 , 一艘船 , 一台拖網 , 一台繪製機器 , 和一台冷藏的機器 。
and my intention was to go out to the gyre , raise awareness about this issue and begin to pick up the plastic , chip it into little bits and cold mold it into bricks that could potentially be used as building materials in underdeveloped communities .	而我的意圖是去蓋瑞 , 提高對這個議題的認知 , 開始把塑膠晶片切成一塊塊又冷的磚塊 , 可以被用來當作被開發出來的材料 。
i began talking with people who actually had been out to the gyre and were studying the plastic problem in the marine environment and upon doing so , i realized actually that cleaning it up would be a very small drop in the bucket relative to how much is being generated every day around the world , and that actually i needed to back up and look at the bigger picture .	我開始和那些真的去過健身房的人談話 , 他們在海洋環境中研究塑膠問題 , 後來我意識到 , 清理塑膠會是一個非常小的滴落在垃圾桶裡 , 與全世界每天產生的成效有關 , 我需要回頭看更大的景象 。
and the bigger picture is: we need to find a way to turn off the faucet .	更大的圖片是:我們需要找到一個方法來關掉這個棚戶 。
we need to cut the spigot of singleuse and disposable plastics , which are entering the marine environment every day on a global scale .	我們需要切斷單一用途和無形塑膠的位置 , 每天都要進入海洋環境 。
so in looking at that , i also realized that i was really angry .	所以 , 仔細看 , 我也發現我很生氣 。
i wasn't just concerned about plastic that you're trying to imagine out in the middle of the pacific ocean of which i have learned there are now 11 gyres , potentially , of plastic in five major oceans in the world .	我不只在乎塑膠 , 你要試著想像在太平洋的中央 , 我發現現在有11個塑膠在世界上五個主要海洋中 。
it's not just that gyre of plastic that i'm concerned about it's the gyre of plastic in the supermarket .	不只是我關心的塑膠薄片 , 它是超市的塑膠環 。
i'd go to the supermarket and all of my food is packaged in plastic .	我會去超市 , 我的所有食物都是塑膠包裝的 。
all of my beverages are packaged in plastic , even at the health food market .	我所有的飲料都包裹在塑膠上 , 甚至在健康的食物市場 。
i'm also concerned about the plastic in the refrigerator , and i'm concerned about the plastic and the toxins that leach from plastic into us and into our bodies .	我也關心冰箱裡的塑膠 , 我關心冰箱裡的塑膠和毒素 , 從塑膠帶到我們體內的毒素 。
so i came together with a group of other people who were all looking at this issue , and we created the plastic pollution coalition .	所以我和一群人一起研究這個問題 , 我們創造了塑膠污染聯盟 。
we have many initiatives that we're working on , but some of them are very basic .	我們有許多我們正在努力的計畫 , 但其中有些很基本 。
one is: if 80 to 90 percent of what we're finding in the ocean of the marine debris that we're finding in the ocean is plastic , then why don't we call it what it is .	第一:如果我們發現海洋碎片的百分之八十到九十 , 我們在海洋中發現的就是塑膠 , 那麼為什麼我們不把它稱為它是什麼 。
recycling everybody kind of ends their books about being sustainable and greening with the idea of recycling .	回收讓每個人都終止了他們的書 , 內容是關於永續和綠化 , 關於回收的概念 。
you put something in a bin and you don't have to think about it again .	你把某樣東西放在一個賓箱裡 , 你不需要再考慮它 。
what is the reality of that ?	真相是什麼 ?
in the united states , less than seven percent of our plastics are recycled .	在美國 , 少於百分之七的塑膠被回收 。
and if you really look into it , particularly when it comes to plastic bottles , most of it is only downcycled , or incinerated , or shipped to china .	如果你真的仔細觀察 , 尤其是對塑膠瓶來說 , 大部份的瓶子只會被循環 , 或被切斷 , 或運送到中國 。
it is downcycled and turned into lesser things , while a glass bottle can be a glass bottle again or can be used again a plastic bottle can never be a plastic bottle again .	它是被循環的 , 轉變為比較少的東西 , 而玻璃瓶可以再次使用玻璃瓶 , 或者再次使用塑膠瓶 , 再也不會再是塑膠瓶 。
so this is a big issue for us .	這對我們來說是個大問題 。
another thing that we're looking at and asking people to think about is we've added a fourth r onto the front of the " reduce , reuse , recycle , " three r's , and that is refuse .	另一個我們正在研究並要求大家思考的是我們把第四個圈子加到 「 減量、再利用、回收 」 、 「 三r 」 的前面 , 那就是拒絕 。
whenever possible , refuse singleuse and disposable plastics .	不論何時 , 只要能拒絕單一用途和可丟棄的塑膠 。
alternatives exist ; some of them are very oldschool .	替代方案存在 ; 有些則是非常古老的學者 。
i myself am now collecting these cool pyrex containers and using those instead of glad and tupperware containers to store food in .	我現在正在收集這些很酷的鳳凰容器 , 用這些東西 , 而不是很高興和超級水華容器來儲存食物 。
and i know that i am doing a service to myself and my family .	我知道我在為自己和家人服務 。
it's very easy to pick up a stainlesssteel bottle or a glass bottle , if you're traveling and you've forgotten to bring your stainlesssteel bottle and fill that up with water or filtered water , versus purchasing plastic bottled water .	很容易拿起一瓶水 , 或一瓶玻璃瓶 , 如果你在旅行 , 你忘了帶著你的永續瓶子 , 填滿水或過濾水 , 和購買塑膠瓶的水 。
i guess what i want to say to everybody here and i know that you guys know a lot about this issue is that this is a huge problem in the oceans , but this is a problem that we've created as consumers and we can solve .	我想對這裡的每一個人說些話我知道你們對這個問題很瞭解這在海洋裡是個大問題但我們以消費者為主我們可以解決這個問題
we can solve this by raising awareness of the issue and teaching people to choose alternatives .	我們可以藉由提高對這個問題的意識 , 並教導人們選擇替代方案 。
so whenever possible , to choose alternatives to singleuse plastics .	所以 , 不論何時 , 要選擇單一用途塑膠的替代方案 。
we can cut the stem tide the stem of this into our oceans and in doing so , save our oceans , save our planet , save ourselves .	我們可以把幹細胞切割成我們的海洋 , 這麼做 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的地球 , 拯救我們自己 。
this demo from pattie maes' lab at mit , spearheaded by pranav mistry was the buzz of ted . it's a wearable device with a projector that paves the way for profound interaction with our environment . imagine " minority report " and then some .	這位來自麻省理工學院的帕蒂•馬賽斯實驗室 , 由帕拉夫•梅雷雷雷雷雷迪推出的展示 , 是ted的buzz 。 這是一個可以穿戴的裝置 , 讓投影機與我們的環境互動 。 想像 「 少數性報告 」 和一些人 。
demo , design , interface design , technology	民主、設計、介面設計、科技、科技、
pattie maes and pranav mistry demo sixthsense	pattiemaes和prantrydemo6ensethesethesethesemes和prantry 。
i've been intrigued by this question of whether we could evolve or develop a sixth sense a sense that would give us seamless access and easy access to metainformation or information that may exist somewhere that may be relevant to help us make the right decision about whatever it is that we're coming across .	我對這個問題很有興趣 , 探討是否能演化或發展出六種感官 , 能給我們安全、容易取得的資訊 , 或可能存在的資訊 , 來協助我們做出正確的決定 。
and some of you may argue , well , don't today's cell phones do that already ?	你們當中有些人可能會爭辯 , 嗯 , 今天的手機已經做到了嗎 ?
but i would say no .	但我會說不 。
when you meet someone here at ted and this is the top networking place , of course , of the year you don't shake somebody's hand and then say , " can you hold on for a moment while i take out my phone and google you ? "	當你在ted見面的時候 , 這當然是網絡最高的地方 , 你不會握某人的手 , 然後說: 「 你能不能在我拿出手機和谷歌的時候握住一會兒 ? 」
or when you go to the supermarket and you're standing there in that huge aisle of different types of toilet papers , you don't take out your cell phone , and open a browser , and go to a website to try to decide which of these different toilet papers is the most ecologically responsible purchase to make .	或者當你去超市時 , 你站在那邊 , 大大大的衛生紙 , 你不會拿出你的手機 , 打開瀏覽器 , 到一個網站 , 試著判斷這些不同的衛生紙是最環保的購買 。
so we don't really have easy access to all this relevant information that can just help us make optimal decisions about what to do next and what actions to take .	所以 , 我們並不容易取得所有相關的資訊 , 能協助我們做出最佳決定 , 來決定下一步要做什麼、採取什麼行動 。
and so my research group at the media lab has been developing a series of inventions to give us access to this information in a sort of easy way , without requiring that the user changes any of their behavior .	所以我在媒體實驗室的研究團隊開發了一系列的發明 , 以一種簡單的方式 , 不需要使用使用者改變他們的行為 。
and i'm here to unveil our latest effort , and most successful effort so far , which is still very much a work in process .	我來這裡是要揭開我們最新的努力 , 目前最成功的努力 , 這仍然是一個過程 。
i'm actually wearing the device right now and we've sort of cobbled it together with components that are off the shelf and that , by the way , only cost 350 dollars at this point in time .	我現在戴著這個裝置 , 我們把它和架上的零件結合在一起 , 順道一提 , 目前只花費350美元 。
i'm wearing a camera , just a simple webcam , a portable , batterypowered projection system with a little mirror .	我戴了一台相機 , 只是個簡單的網路攝影機 , 一個可攜帶、電力投影系統 , 裡面有一面鏡子 。
these components communicate to my cell phone in my pocket which acts as the communication and computation device .	這些元件在我的口袋裡傳達我的手機 , 它扮演了通訊和計算裝置 。
and in the video here we see my student pranav mistry , who's really the genius who's been implementing and designing this whole system .	在這段影片中 , 我們看到我的學生帕拉夫•梅瑞瑞 , 他真的在執行和設計整個系統的天才 。
and we see how this system lets him walk up to any surface and start using his hands to interact with the information that is projected in front of him .	我們看到這個系統讓他走到任何表面 , 開始使用他的雙手 , 來和他前面的資訊互動 。
the system tracks the four significant fingers .	系統追蹤了四個重要的手指 。
in this case , he's wearing simple marker caps that you may recognize .	在這個例子中 , 他戴著你可能認出的簡單筆蓋 。
but if you want a more stylish version you could also paint your nails in different colors .	但如果你想要更堅固的版本 , 你也可以用不同顏色來畫指甲 。
and the camera basically tracks these four fingers and recognizes any gestures that he's making so he can just go to , for example , a map of long beach , zoom in and out , etc .	相機基本上會追蹤這四隻手指 , 然後辨識出他所做的任何姿勢 , 例如 , 他可以直接去看一張長灘的地圖 , 放大 , 等等 。
the system also recognizes iconic gestures such as the " take a picture " gesture , and then takes a picture of whatever is in front of you .	系統也能辨識出 「 拍照 」 的標誌姿勢 , 然後拍下你面前的任何東西 。
and when he then walks back to the media lab , he can just go up to any wall and project all the pictures that he's taken , sort through them and organize them , and resize them , etc . , again using all natural gestures .	當他走回媒體實驗室時 , 他可以走到任何一面牆上 , 把他拍到的所有照片分類 , 組織它們 , 將它們 , 再次使用所有自然的手勢 。
so , some of you most likely were here two years ago and saw the demo by jeff han or some of you may think , " well , doesn't this look like the microsoft surface table ? "	兩年前 , 在座可能有人來這裡看過傑夫•漢的示範 , 或者有些人可能會想: 「 嗯 , 這看起來不像微軟表面桌子嗎 ? 」
and yes , you also interact using natural gestures , both hands , etc .	是的 , 你也用天然手勢 , 雙手 , 等等 。
but the difference here is that you can use any surface , you can walk to up to any surface , including your hand if nothing else is available and interact with this projected data .	但差別在於 , 你可以用任何表面 , 你可以走到任何表面 , 包括你的手 , 如果沒有任何東西可以使用 , 並和這個投影資料互動 。
the device is completely portable , and can be . . .	這個裝置是完全可攜帶的 , 可以是......
so one important difference is that it's totally mobile .	其中一個很重要的差異是它完全是移動的 。
another even more important difference is that in mass production this would not cost more tomorrow than today's cell phones and would actually not sort of be a bigger packaging could look a lot more stylish than this version that i'm wearing around my neck .	另一個更重要的差異是 , 在大規模生產 , 比現在的手機還要多 , 實際上 , 不是更大的包裝 , 會比我在脖子上穿著的這個版本更加風格 。
but other than letting some of you live out your fantasy of looking as cool as tom cruise in " minority report , " the reason why we're really excited about this device is that it really can act as one of these sixthsense devices that gives you relevant information about whatever is in front of you .	但 , 除了讓你們當中一些人想出來的幻想 , 像湯姆•克魯塞在《少數報告》中 , 我們真的很興奮的原因是 , 它能做出第六感的裝置 , 讓你對於你面前的任何相關資訊 。
so we see pranav here going into the supermarket and he's shopping for some paper towels .	我們看到帕拉夫走進超市 , 他購買了一些紙巾 。
and , as he picks up a product the system can recognize the product that he's picking up , using either image recognition or marker technology , and give him the green light or an orange light .	當他拿起一個產品時 , 這個系統可以辨識出他拿出來的產品 , 不論是圖像辨識或標記技術 , 給他綠光或橘光 。
he can ask for additional information .	他可以請求額外的資訊 。
so this particular choice here is a particularly good choice , given his personal criteria .	所以這個選擇是特別好的選擇 , 因為他的個人標準 。
some of you may want the toilet paper with the most bleach in it rather than the most ecologicallyresponsible choice .	有些人可能想要馬桶紙 , 上面有最多漏洞 , 而不是最環保的選擇 。
if he picks up a book in the bookstore , he can get an amazon rating it gets projected right on the cover of the book .	如果他在書店裡拿起一本書 , 他就能得到亞馬遜評級 , 會直接投入書的封面 。
this is juan's book , our previous speaker , which gets a great rating , by the way , at amazon .	這是朱恩的書 , 我們之前的講者 , 可以得到很棒的評分 , 順帶一提 , 在亞馬遜 。
and so , pranav turns the page of the book and can then see additional information about the book reader comments , maybe sort of information by his favorite critic , etc .	所以 , 帕拉夫把書本的頁面轉換成可以看到更多關於讀者評論的信息 , 或許他最喜歡的評論家等等 。
if he turns to a particular page he finds an annotation by maybe an expert of a friend of ours that gives him a little bit of additional information about whatever is on that particular page .	如果他轉到一個特定的頁面 , 他可能是一位朋友的專家 , 他給他一些額外的資訊 , 給他一些特定頁面上的任何東西 。
reading the newspaper it never has to be outdated .	閱讀報紙從來不需要太過期 。
you can get video annotations of the event that you're reading about you can get the latest sports scores etc .	你可以收到關於你所讀到的事件的記錄 , 你可以得到最新的運動分數 。
this is a more controversial one .	這是一個比較有爭議的 。
as you interact with someone at ted , maybe you can see a word cloud of the tags , the words that are associated with that person in their blog and personal web pages .	當你和ted的人互動時 , 也許你能看到標籤的一個字雲 , 和那個人的部落格和個人網頁相關的詞彙 。
in this case , the student is interested in cameras , etc .	在這個例子中 , 學生對攝影機有興趣 , 等等 。
on your way to the airport , if you pick up your boarding pass , it can tell you that your flight is delayed , that the gate has changed , etc .	在你去機場的路上 , 如果你拿起你的登機車 , 它可以告訴你 , 你的航班延遲 , 大門已經改變了 , 等等 。
and , if you need to know what the current time is it's as simple as drawing a watch on your arm .	如果你需要知道當下的時間 , 它就像在手臂上畫手錶一樣簡單 。
so that's where we're at so far in developing this sixth sense that would give us seamless access to all this relevant information about the things that we may come across .	所以 , 這就是我們目前正在發展的第六感 , 讓我們能無縫地取得所有相關的資訊 , 關於我們可能碰到的事物 。
my student pranav , who's really , like i said , the genius behind this .	我的學生帕拉夫 , 像我說的 , 他是這背後的天才 。
he does deserve a lot of applause because i don't think he's slept much in the last three months , actually .	他的確值得掌聲 , 因為我認為他在過去三個月中不多睡覺 。
and his girlfriend is probably not very happy about him either .	他的女友可能也不會對他感到高興 。
but it's not perfect yet , it's very much a work in progress .	但它尚未完美 , 它是進步的一份工作 。
and who knows , maybe in another 10 years we'll be here with the ultimate sixth sense brain implant .	誰知道 , 或許在十年後 , 我們會帶著最後的第六種感官植入腦內 。
phyllis rodriguez and aicha elwafi have a powerful friendship born of unthinkable loss . rodriguez' son was killed in the world trade center attacks on september 11 , 2001 ; elwafi's son zacarias moussaoui was convicted of a role in those attacks and is serving a life sentence . in hoping to find peace , these two moms have come to understand and respect one another .	菲莉絲•羅德里格和艾瑞克•勞德里格 , 有一個很有力的友誼 , 出自於世貿中心的兒子 , 在2001年9月11日被殺害 , 伊波菲的兒子薩洛伊被定罪在這些攻擊中 , 被定罪 , 希望能找到和平的句子 。 這兩個母親也開始了解並尊重另一個 。
culture , global issues , politics	文化、全球議題、政治、
9/11 healing: the mothers who found forgiveness , friendship	9/11的治療:那些發現寬恕的母親 , 友誼 , 友誼 。
phyllis rodriguez: we are here today because of the fact that we have what most people consider an unusual friendship .	菲莉絲•羅德里格茲:我們今天來到這裡 , 是因為我們大部份人認為這種不尋常的友誼 。
and yet , it feels natural to us now .	但 , 現在感覺很自然 。
i first learned that my son had been in the world trade center on the morning of september 11th , 2001 .	我第一次發現 , 我的兒子在2001年9月11日的早晨在世界貿易中心 。
we didn't know if he had perished yet until 36 hours later .	我們不知道他是否過世直到36個小時後
at the time , we knew that it was political .	當時 , 我們知道那是政治的 。
we were afraid of what our country was going to do in the name of our son my husband , orlando , and i and our family .	我們害怕我們的國家將以我們兒子的名字來做些什麼 , 我的丈夫奧蘭多 , 我和我們的家人 。
and when i saw it and yet , through the shock , the terrible shock , and the terrible explosion in our lives , literally , we were not vengeful .	當我看到這個震驚時 , 可怕的震驚 , 我們生命中可怕的爆炸 , 真的是 , 我們沒有復仇 。
and a couple of weeks later when zacarias moussaoui was indicted on six counts of conspiracy to commit terrorism , and the u . s . government called for a death penalty for him , if convicted , my husband and i spoke out in opposition to that , publicly .	幾個星期後 , zacariasmosaoui被指出六個對恐怖主義的陰謀 , 而美國政府要求對他做死刑 , 如果被定罪 , 我的丈夫和我公開對立的對話 。
through that and through human rights groups , we were brought together with several other victims' families .	透過人權團體 , 我們和其他幾個受害者的家庭聚在一起 。
when i saw aicha in the media , coming over when her son was indicted , and i thought , " what a brave woman .	當我在媒體上看到aicha , 她兒子被指控時 , 我心想: 「 勇敢的女人 。
someday i want to meet that woman when i'm stronger . "	有一天 , 我想要見到那個女人 , 當我更強壯的時候 。 」
i was still in deep grief ; i knew i didn't have the strength .	我仍然處在悲慟深處 , 我知道我沒有力量 。
i knew i would find her someday , or we would find each other .	我知道有一天我會找到她 , 或找到彼此 。
because , when people heard that my son was a victim , i got immediate sympathy .	因為 , 當人們聽到我兒子是受害者時 , 我馬上就有同情心了 。
but when people learned what her son was accused of , she didn't get that sympathy .	但當人們知道她的兒子被指控時 , 她沒有得到同情 。
but her suffering is equal to mine .	但她的苦難和我的苦難 。
so we met in november 2002 , and aicha will now tell you how that came about .	我們在2002年11月見面 , aicha現在會告訴你這是怎麼來的 。
aicha elwafi: good afternoon , ladies and gentlemen .	aichaelwafi:午安 , 女士們先生們 。
i am the mother of zacarias moussaoui .	我是zacariamosaoui的母親 。
and i asked the organization of human rights to put me in touch with the parents of the victims .	我請人權組織把我和受害者的父母聯繫起來 。
so they introduced me to five families .	所以他們介紹我到五個家庭 。
and i saw phyllis , and i watched her .	我看到phyllis , 看著她 。
she was the only mother in the group .	她是團體中唯一的母親 。
the others were brothers , sisters .	其他人則是兄弟姊妹 。
and i saw in her eyes that she was a mother , just like me .	我在她眼中看到 , 她是母親 , 就像我一樣 。
i suffered a lot as a mother .	身為母親 , 我遭受了很多苦難 。
i was married when i was 14 .	我14歲就結婚了 。
i lost a child when i was 15 , a second child when i was 16 .	我十五歲時失去了一個孩子 , 一個十六歲的第二個孩子 。
so the story with zacarias was too much really .	zacaria的故事實在太多了 。
and i still suffer , because my son is like he's buried alive .	我仍然會受苦 , 因為我的兒子就像被埋葬了 。
i know she really cried for her son .	我知道她真的為她的兒子哭了 。
but she knows where he is .	但她知道他在哪裡 。
my son , i don't know where he is .	我兒子不知道他在哪裡 。
i don't know if he's alive . i don't know if he's tortured .	我不知道他是否活著 。 我不知道他是否被折磨 。
i don't know what happened to him .	我不知道他怎麼了 。
so that's why i decided to tell my story , so that my suffering is something positive for other women .	這就是為什麼我決定要說我的故事 , 所以我的苦難對其他女性來說是很正面的 。
for all the women , all the mothers that give life , you can give back , you can change .	對所有婦女來說 , 給予生命的所有母親 , 你可以回饋 , 你可以改變 。
it's up to us women , because we are women , because we love our children .	由於我們是女性 , 因為我們是女性 , 因為我們愛我們的孩子 。
we must be handinhand and do something together .	我們必須親手做點什麼 。
it's not against women , it's for us , for us women , for our children .	不是反對女性 , 而是為了我們女性 , 為我們的孩子 。
i talk against violence , against terrorism .	我談到暴力 , 反對恐怖主義 。
i go to schools to talk to young , muslim girls so they don't accept to be married against their will very young .	我去學校和年輕的穆斯林女孩談話 , 這樣她們不接受結婚 , 會很年輕 。
so if i can save one of the young girls , and avoid that they get married and suffer as much as i did , well this is something good .	所以 , 如果我能拯救其中一個年輕女孩 , 避免她們結婚並受苦 , 像我一樣 , 這是件好事 。
this is why i'm here in front of you .	這就是為什麼我站在你們面前 。
pr: i would like to say that i have learned so much from aicha , starting with that day we had our very first meeting with other family members which was a very private meeting with security , because it was november 2002 , and , frankly , we were afraid of the superpatriotism of that time in the country those of us family members .	pr:我想要說 , 我從aicha學到很多 , 從那天開始 , 我們和其他家庭成員第一次見面 , 那是個非常私密的會議 , 因為那是2002年11月 , 坦白說 , 我們害怕當時在美國家庭成員的超級病態 。
but we were all so nervous .	但我們都很緊張 。
" why does she want to meet us ? "	「 為什麼她想要見我們 ? 」
and then she was nervous .	然後她很緊張 。
" why did we want to meet her ? "	「 為什麼我們想要見她 ? 」
what did we want from each other ?	我們彼此想要什麼 ?
before we knew each others' names , or anything , we had embraced and wept .	在我們認識彼此的名字之前 , 或任何東西 , 我們都很擁抱和哭泣 。
then we sat in a circle with support , with help , from people experienced in this kind of reconciliation .	然後我們就坐在一個充滿支持的圈子裡 , 帶著幫助 , 從人們體驗到這種協調 。
and aicha started , and she said , " i don't know if my son is guilty or innocent , but i want to tell you how sorry i am for what happened to your families .	aicha開始 , 她說: 「 我不知道我的兒子是有罪或無辜 , 但我想告訴你們 , 我對你的家庭發生了多麼的抱歉 。
i know what it is to suffer , and i feel that if there is a crime , a person should be tried fairly and punished . "	我知道痛苦是什麼 , 我覺得如果有犯罪 , 一個人應該要被懲罰 。 」
but she reached out to us in that way , and it was , i'd like to say , it was an icebreaker .	但她以這種方式向我們伸出援手 , 我想要說 , 那是個冰箱 。
and what happened then is we all told our stories , and we all connected as human beings .	接下來發生的是 , 我們都說自己的故事 , 我們都以人類的身分連結在一起 。
by the end of the afternoon it was about three hours after lunch we'd felt as if we'd known each other forever .	下午結束後 , 午餐後的三小時 , 感覺好像我們永遠認識對方 。
now what i learned from her , is a woman , not only who could be so generous under these present circumstances and what it was then , and what was being done to her son , but the life she's had .	我從她身上學到的是 , 一個女人 , 不只是在這些現狀下 , 還有當時的一切 , 還有她兒子的人生 。
i never had met someone with such a hard life , from such a totally different culture and environment from my own .	我從來沒有遇過這麼辛苦的人生 , 來自完全不同的文化和環境 。
and i feel that we have a special connection , which i value very much .	我覺得我們有一個特殊的連結 , 我非常重視它 。
and i think it's all about being afraid of the other , but making that step and then realizing , " hey , this wasn't so hard .	我想 , 重點是要害怕另一方 , 但要踏出那一步 , 然後意識到: 「 嘿 , 這並不難 。
who else can i meet that i don't know , or that i'm so different from ? "	還有誰能見到我不知道的 , 還是我和他很不一樣 ? 」
so , aicha , do you have a couple of words for conclusion ?	所以 , aicha , 你有幾個字來做結論嗎 ?
because our time is up .	因為我們的時間到了 。

this is what i wanted to say .	這是我想要說的 。

now i see you've all been enjoying the water that's been provided for you here at the conference , over the past couple of days .	現在我看到你們都很享受這場研討會的水 。 過去幾天來 , 你們都很享受這場演說 。
and i'm sure you'll feel that it's from a safe source .	我相信你們會覺得這來自安全的來源 。
but what if it wasn't ?	但如果不是呢 ?
what if it was from a source like this ?	如果是像這樣的來源呢 ?
then statistics would actually say that half of you would now be suffering with diarrhea .	接著 , 統計數字會說 , 你們當中有一半的人會遭受腹瀉 。
i talked a lot in the past about statistics , and the provision of safe drinking water for all .	過去我談了很多關於統計 , 以及所有人的安全飲用水 。
but they just don't seem to get through .	但他們似乎不會經歷 。
and i think i've worked out why .	我想我已經知道為什麼 。
it's because , using current thinking , the scale of the problem just seems too huge to contemplate solving .	因為 , 利用目前的思維 , 問題的規模似乎太大 , 無法思考解決問題 。
so we just switch off: us , governments and aid agencies .	所以我們就關掉:我們、政府和援助機構 。
well , today , i'd like to show you that through thinking differently , the problem has been solved .	今天 , 我想用不同的方式來說明 , 問題已經解決了 。
by the way , since i've been speaking , another 13 , 000 people around the world are suffering now with diarrhea .	順帶一提 , 自從我說話之後 , 全世界還有一萬三千人正在受腹瀉所苦 。
and four children have just died .	四個孩子剛過世 。
i invented lifesaver bottle because i got angry .	我發明了救生瓶 , 因為我生氣了 。
i , like most of you , was sitting down , the day after christmas in 2004 , when i was watching the devastating news of the asian tsunami as it rolled in , playing out on tv .	我跟你們一樣 , 在2004年聖誕節後的那一天 , 我看著亞洲海嘯爆炸的消息 , 在電視上播放 。
the days and weeks that followed , people fleeing to the hills , being forced to drink contaminated water or face death .	接下來的幾天 , 人們逃到山上 , 被迫飲用污染的水或死亡 。
that really stuck with me .	這真的困住了我 。
then , a few months later , hurricane katrina slammed into the side of america .	接著 , 幾個月後 , 卡崔娜颶風溜到美國 。
" okay , " i thought , " here's a first world country , let's see what they can do . "	我心想: 「 好吧 , 這裡是第一個國家 , 讓我們看看他們能做些什麼 。 」
do you know it took five days to get water to the superdome ?	你知道花了五天才把水送到超級質數上嗎 ?
people were shooting each other on the streets for tv sets and water .	人們在街上互相射擊 , 為電視和水照射 。
that's when i decided i had to do something .	那時我決定要做點什麼 。
now i spent a lot of time in my garage , over the next weeks and months , and also in my kitchen much to the dismay of my wife .	我花了很多時間在我的車庫裡 , 在接下來的幾週、幾個月 , 在我妻子的廚房裡 , 我也在廚房裡待了很多時間 。
however , after a few failed prototypes , i finally came up with this , the lifesaver bottle .	然而 , 在幾次失敗的原型之後 , 我終於想出了這個 , 救生瓶 。
okay , now for the science bit .	好 , 現在來談科學 。
before lifesaver , the best hand filters were only capable of filtering down to about 200 nanometers .	在生命saver之前 , 最好的過濾器只能過濾到大約200奈米 。
the smallest bacteria is about 200 nanometers .	最小的細菌大約是200奈米 。
so a 200nanometer bacteria is going to get through a 200nanometer hole .	一個200奈米的細菌會穿過200奈米的洞 。
the smallest virus , on the other hand , is about 25 nanometers .	另一方面 , 最小的病毒大約是25奈米 。
so that's definitely going to get through those 200 nanometer holes .	這肯定會穿過那200奈米的洞 。
lifesaver pores are 15 nanometers .	救生器是15奈米長 。
so nothing is getting through .	所以 , 沒有什麼事情會發生 。
okay , i'm going to give you a bit of a demonstration .	好 , 我要給你們一些示範 。
would you like to see that ?	你們想要看到嗎 ?
i spent all the time setting this up , so i guess i should .	我一直都在設定它 , 所以我猜我應該要 。

so someone's done that up .	有人這樣做 。
fine city of oxford , so what i've done is i've gone and got some water from the river cherwell , and the river thames , that flow through here . and this is the water .	牛津的好城市 , 我做的是 , 我從河流cherwell取得一些水 , 還有河流 , 流過這裡 。 這就是水 。
but i got to thinking , you know , if we were in the middle of a flood zone in bangladesh , the water wouldn't look like this .	但我必須想 , 如果我們在孟加拉的洪水區中間 , 水就不會像這樣 。
so i've gone and got some stuff to add into it .	所以 , 我已經有了一些東西來加入它 。
and this is from my pond .	這是我的池塘 。
have a smell of that , mister cameraman .	聞一下 , 攝影師 。
we're just going to pour that in there .	我們只會把它倒進去 。
michael pritchard: okay . we've got some runoff from a sewage plant farm .	michaelpritchard:好的 , 我們有一些從污水農田中跑出來的 。
so i'm just going to put that in there .	所以 , 我要把它放進去 。
put that in there . there we go .	把它放進去 。 開始 。
and some other bits and pieces , chuck that in there .	還有其他的部份和碎片 , 把它切進去 。
and i've got a gift here from a friend of mine's rabbit .	我有個來自我的朋友的兔子 。
so we're just going to put that in there as well .	所以 , 我們也要把它放進去 。
the lifesaver bottle works really simply .	救生瓶真的很簡單 。
you just scoop the water up .	你只要把水趕上來 。
today i'm going to use a jug just to show you all . let's get a bit of that poo in there .	今天我要用一個袋子給你們看 。 讓我們看看裡面的一小塊 。
that's not dirty enough . let's just stir that up a little bit .	那還不夠髒 。 讓我們稍微攪拌一下 。
okay , so i'm going to take this really filthy water , and put it in here . do you want a drink yet ?	好吧 , 我要用這個非常骯髒的水 , 把它放到這裡 , 你還想要喝杯嗎 ?
okay . there we go .	好 , 開始了 。
give it a few pumps . okay ?	給它一些幫浦 。 好嗎 ?
that's all that's necessary .	這些都是必要的 。
now as soon as i pop the teat , sterile drinking water is going to come out .	一旦我穿著茶的時候 , 無菌飲用水就會出現 。
i've got to be quick . okay , ready ?	我得快點 。 好 , 準備好了嗎 ?
there we go . mind the electrics .	開始了 。 請注意電源 。
that is safe , sterile drinking water .	那很安全 , 無菌飲用水 。
there you go chris .	克里斯 。
what's it taste of ?	它的味道是什麼 ?
let's see chris's program throughout the rest of the show . okay ?	咱們來看看克里斯的節目在整個節目的其他部分 。 好嗎 ?
okay . lifesaver bottle is used by thousands of people around the world .	好吧 , 世界各地數以千計的人使用生命瓶 。
it'll last for 6 , 000 liters .	它會維持六千公升 。
and when it's expired , using failsafe technology , the system will shut off , protecting the user .	當它被激發時 , 使用失敗的技術 , 系統會停止 , 保護使用者 。
pop the cartridge out . pop a new one in .	把地毯放出來 , 再放一個新的 。
it's good for another 6 , 000 liters .	另外六千公升是好的 。
so let's look at the applications .	咱們來看看應用程式 。
traditionally , in a crisis , what do we do ?	傳統上 , 在危機中 , 我們該怎麼做 ?
then , after a few weeks , we set up camps .	幾週後 , 我們成立營地 。
and people are forced to come into the camps to get their safe drinking water .	人們被迫進入難民營 , 以取得安全的飲用水 。
what happens when 20 , 000 people congregate in a camp ?	當兩萬人聚集在營地時會發生什麼事 ?
diseases spread . more resources are required .	疾病散播 。 需要更多的資源 。
the problem just becomes selfperpetuating .	問題就在於自我繁榮 。
but by thinking differently , and shipping these , people can stay put .	但用不同的方式思考 , 運送這些 , 人們可以留下 。
they can make their own sterile drinking water , and start to get on with rebuilding their homes and their lives .	他們可以製造自己的無菌飲用水 , 開始重建家園和生活 。
now , it doesn't require a natural disaster for this to work .	這並不需要天然災難才能成功 。
using the old thinking , of national infrastructure and pipe work , is too expensive .	用舊的想法 , 國家基礎建設和管道工作太昂貴了 。
when you run the numbers on a calculator , you run out of noughts .	當你在計算機上運算數字時 , 你就會跑出音符 。
so here is the " thinking different " bit .	這就是 「 不同的思考 」 的部分 。
instead of shipping water , and using manmade processes to do it , let's use mother nature . she's got a fantastic system .	不用運送水 , 用人造過程來做 , 咱們用大自然 。 她有一個很棒的系統 。
she picks the water up from there , desalinates it , for free , transports it over there , and dumps it onto the mountains , rivers , and streams .	她從那裡撿起水 , 免費運送到那裡 , 把它丟到山上 , 河流和溪流 。
and where do people live ? near water .	人們住在哪裡 ? 靠近水源 。
all we've go to do is make it sterile . how do we do that ?	我們要做的就是讓它變得無效 。 我們該怎麼做 ?
well , we could use the lifesaver bottle .	嗯 , 我們可以用救生瓶 。
or we could use one of these .	或者 , 我們可以用其中一種 。
the same technology , in a jerry can .	同樣的技術 , 在jerry可以 。
this will process 25 , 000 liters of water ; that's good enough for a family of four , for three years .	這個過程會處理2萬5千公升的水 ; 這足夠給一個四個、三年的家庭 。
and how much does it cost ?	要花多少錢 ?
about half a cent a day to run .	每天大約花半分錢去跑 。
so , by thinking differently , and processing water at the point of use , mothers and children no longer have to walk four hours a day to collect their water .	所以 , 用不同的方式思考 , 處理水 , 母親和孩子不再需要每天四個小時來收集他們的水 。
they can get it from a source nearby .	它們可以從附近的來源取得 。
so with just eight billion dollars , we can hit the millennium goal's target of halving the number of people without access to safe drinking water .	只有八十億美金 , 我們就能達到千禧目標的目標 , 無法取得安全飲用水的目標 。
to put that into context , the u . k . government spends about 12 billion pounds a year on foreign aid .	要把這句話說成 , 英國政府每年花費大約120億英鎊在國外援助 。
but why stop there ?	但為什麼要停在那裡 ?
with 20 billion dollars , everyone can have access to safe drinking water .	有了2000億美元 , 每個人都可以取得安全的飲用水 。
so the threeandahalf billion people that suffer every year as a result , and the two million kids that die every year , will live .	所以每年有三十五億人受苦 , 每年有兩百萬名孩童會活下來 。
paddy ashdown claims that we are living in a moment in history where power is changing in ways it never has before . in a spellbinding talk at tedxbrussels he outlines the three major global shifts that he sees coming .	帕迪阿許諾聲明 , 我們生活在歷史上的一個時刻 , 權力從來沒有改變過 。 在tedxbrussel的拼寫演說中 , 他推出了三個主要的全球轉變 。
foreign policy , global issues , politics , world cultures	外交政策、全球議題、政治、世界文化文化、外交政策、全球議題、政治、世界文化、文化 。
paddy ashdown: the global power shift	paddyashown:全球的權力轉移 。
there's a poem written by a very famous english poet at the end of the 19th century .	在19世紀末 , 有一首詩寫了一首有名的英文詩 。
it was said to echo in churchill's brain in the 1930s .	在1930年代 , 它被告知在教堂的大腦 。
and the poem goes: " on the idle hill of summer , lazy with the flow of streams , hark i hear a distant drummer , drumming like a sound in dreams , far and near and low and louder on the roads of earth go by , dear to friend and food to powder , soldiers marching , soon to die . "	這首詩說: " 在夏天的河床上 , 懶惰著河流 , 我聽到遠方的鼓聲 , 像在夢裡的聲音 , 距離很遠、很低、很大聲 , 在地球的道路上 , 親愛的朋友和食物到粉末 , 士兵們很快就死了 。 "
those who are interested in poetry , the poem is " a shropshire lad " written by a . e . housman .	那些對詩有興趣的人 , 這首詩是《shropshirelad》 , 由a.housman寫的 。
but what housman understood , and you hear it in the symphonies of nielsen too , was that the long , hot , silvan summers of stability of the 19th century were coming to a close , and that we were about to move into one of those terrifying periods of history when power changes .	但 , 休士曼明白的 , 你也在尼爾森的交響曲中聽到 , 那就是十九世紀的長期、炎熱、銀的穩定夏天即將接近 , 我們即將進入歷史的一個令人害怕的時代 。
and these are always periods , ladies and gentlemen , accompanied by turbulence , and all too often by blood .	各位先生女士 , 這些都是亂流的時期 , 通常是血液循環 。
and my message for you is that i believe we are condemned , if you like , to live at just one of those moments in history when the gimbals upon which the established order of power is beginning to change and the new look of the world , the new powers that exist in the world , are beginning to take form .	我告訴你們的是 , 我相信我們是被拘束的 , 如果你喜歡 , 生活在歷史上的其中一個時刻 , 當權力的基礎開始改變 , 世界存在的新勢力開始形成 。
and these are and we see it very clearly today nearly always highly turbulent times , highly difficult times , and all too often very bloody times .	而我們今天看到的這些是非常明顯的 , 幾乎總是高度的亂流、高度困難的時代 , 很多時候都太血腥了 。
by the way , it happens about once every century .	順帶一提 , 它每世紀都會發生一次 。
you might argue that the last time it happened and that's what housman felt coming and what churchill felt too was that when power passed from the old nations , the old powers of europe , across the atlantic to the new emerging power of the united states of america the beginning of the american century .	你可能會認為 , 上次發生的那段時間 , 休士曼的感受到的 , 以及教堂的感受也一樣 , 當權力從舊國家傳遞 , 歐洲的舊勢力 , 橫跨大西洋 , 到美國一開始的新興力量 。
and of course , into the vacuum where the tooold european powers used to be were played the two bloody catastrophes of the last century the one in the first part and the one in the second part: the two great world wars .	當然 , 在真空中 , 以前歐洲的權力在上個世紀的兩場血腥災難 , 第一部分和第二部分:世界大戰 。
mao zedong used to refer to them as the european civil wars , and it's probably a more accurate way of describing them .	毛澤東曾經稱之為歐洲內戰 , 它可能是更精確的描述方式 。
well , ladies and gentlemen , we live at one of those times .	各位先生女士 , 我們生活在其中之一 。
but for us , i want to talk about three factors today .	但對我們來說 , 我今天想談三個因素 。
and the first of these , the first two of these , is about a shift in power .	第一個是權力的轉變 。
and the second is about some new dimension which i want to refer to , which has never quite happened in the way it's happening now .	第二個是關於一些我想要說的新維度 , 它從來沒有發生過 。
but let's talk about the shifts of power that are occurring to the world .	但 , 讓我們來談談 「 權力 」 的轉變 。
and what is happening today is , in one sense , frightening because it's never happened before .	今天發生的是 , 某種程度上 , 恐怖的原因是 , 以前從來沒有發生過 。
we have seen lateral shifts of power the power of greece passed to rome and the power shifts that occurred during the european civilizations but we are seeing something slightly different .	我們已經看過後續的權力轉變 , 希臘通過羅馬的力量 , 以及在歐洲文明中發生的權力轉變 , 但我們看到了稍微不同的東西 。
for power is not just moving laterally from nation to nation .	對於權力的權力 , 不只是從國家轉移到國家 。
it's also moving vertically .	它也垂直移動 。
what's happening today is that the power that was encased , held to accountability , held to the rule of law , within the institution of the nation state has now migrated in very large measure onto the global stage .	現今的情況是 , 被監禁的力量 , 被責任歸屬於法律的規則 , 在這個國家的制度中 , 現在已經在非常大量的測量上移居到全球階段 。
the globalization of power we talk about the globalization of markets , but actually it's the globalization of real power .	全球化的權力 , 我們談到全球化市場 , 但實際上是全球化的力量 。
and where , at the nation state level that power is held to accountability subject to the rule of law , on the international stage it is not .	在國際上 , 權力的本質是責任制定法律的規則 , 在國際舞台上 , 權力並非如此 。
the international stage and the global stage where power now resides: the power of the internet , the power of the satellite broadcasters , the power of the money changers this vast moneygoround that circulates now 32 times the amount of money necessary for the trade it's supposed to be there to finance the money changers , if you like , the financial speculators that have brought us all to our knees quite recently , the power of the multinational corporations now developing budgets often bigger than mediumsized countries .	國際舞台和國際舞台現在仍然存在:網路的力量 , 衛星廣播的力量 , 金錢改變了這個巨大貨幣的力量 , 現在有32倍的金額 , 供給交易所需的金額 , 應該是為了資助改變者 , 如果你喜歡 , 金融的猜測者 , 最近才把我們全部帶到我們的膝蓋上 , 最大規模的預算能力 , 比原本國家還要大 。
these live in a global space which is largely unregulated , not subject to the rule of law , and in which people may act free of constraint .	這些生活在一個大量未受規範的全球空間中 , 不受法律規範 , 人們可能會自由受限制 。
now that suits the powerful up to a moment .	這種裝置能容納強大的一刻 。
it's always suitable for those who have the most power to operate in spaces without constraint , but the lesson of history is that , sooner or later , unregulated space space not subject to the rule of law becomes populated , not just by the things you wanted international trade , the internet , etc . but also by the things you don't want international criminality , international terrorism .	對於那些擁有最有權力的人 , 在沒有限制的空間中運作 , 但歷史的教訓是 , 不久後 , 不受規範的空間 , 不受法律規範的限制 , 不僅僅是你想要國際貿易、網路等等 。 還有那些你不想要國際犯罪、國際恐怖主義的東西 。
the revelation of 9/11 is that even if you are the most powerful nation on earth , nevertheless , those who inhabit that space can attack you even in your most iconic of cities one bright september morning .	911的揭示是 , 即使你是地球上最強大的國家 , 儘管如此 , 那些住在太空中的人 , 甚至可以攻擊你 , 甚至在9月的早晨 , 一個明亮的城市 。
it's said that something like 60 percent of the four million dollars that was taken to fund 9/11 actually passed through the institutions of the twin towers which 9/11 destroyed .	據說 , 大約百分之六十的四百萬美金被拿來資助9/11的資助機構通過雙胞胎塔破壞的機構 。
you see , our enemies also use this space the space of mass travel , the internet , satellite broadcasters to be able to get around their poison , which is about destroying our systems and our ways .	我們的敵人也使用這個空間--大量旅行、網際網路、衛星廣播 , 能夠在它們的毒害之下逃避我們的系統和方法 。
sooner or later , sooner or later , the rule of history is that where power goes governance must follow .	不久之後 , 不久後 , 歷史的規則是權力的治理必須遵循 。
and if it is therefore the case , as i believe it is , that one of the phenomenon of our time is the globalization of power , then it follows that one of the challenges of our time is to bring governance to the global space .	如果我相信 , 如同我所說的 , 我們這個時代的現象之一就是權力的全球化 , 那麼我們這個時代的挑戰之一就是把統治帶到全球 。
and i believe that the decades ahead of us now will be to a greater or lesser extent turbulent the more or less we are able to achieve that aim: to bring governance to the global space .	我相信 , 未來的幾十年將會變成更大或更少的亂流 , 我們能達成目標:將治理帶給全球空間 。
now notice , i'm not talking about government .	請注意 , 我不是在說政府 。
i'm not talking about setting up some global democratic institution .	我不是要設立一些全球民主制度 。
my own view , by the way , ladies and gentlemen , is that this is unlikely to be done by spawning more u . n . institutions .	順便說一下 , 女士們先生們 , 我自己的觀點是不太可能通過聯合國的更多機構來完成的 。
if we didn't have the u . n . , we'd have to invent it .	如果我們沒有聯合國 , 我們就得發明它 。
the world needs an international forum .	世界需要一個國際論壇 。
it needs a means by which you can legitimize international action .	它需要一種方式來合法化國際行動 。
but when it comes to governance of the global space , my guess is this won't happen through the creation of more u . n . institutions .	但 , 當談到全球空間的治理時 , 我猜這不會發生在聯合國的創建中 。
it will actually happen by the powerful coming together and making treatybased systems , treatybased agreements , to govern that global space .	它實際上會由強而有力的團結組成 , 建立以治療為基礎的系統 , 來治理這個全球空間 。
and if you look , you can see them happening , already beginning to emerge .	如果你看 , 你可以看到他們正在發生 , 已經開始出現了 。
the world trade organization: treatybased organization , entirely treatybased , and yet , powerful enough to hold even the most powerful , the united states , to account if necessary .	世界貿易組織:以條約為基礎的組織 , 完全以治療為基礎 , 但 , 強而有力的組織 , 甚至能夠保持最強大的美國 , 如果需要的話 。
kyoto: the beginnings of struggling to create a treatybased organization .	kyoto:努力創造一個以條約為基礎的組織 。
the g20: we know now that we have to put together an institution which is capable of bringing governance to that financial space for financial speculation .	g20:我們現在知道我們必須建立一個機構 , 能夠將治理帶給金融空間給財務猜測 。
and that's what the g20 is , a treatybased institution .	這就是g20的基礎機構 。
now there's a problem there , and we'll come back to it in a minute , which is that if you bring the most powerful together to make the rules in treatybased institutions , to fill that governance space , then what happens to the weak who are left out ?	這裡有個問題 , 我們等一下會再回來 , 也就是 , 如果你把最強大的力量集合起來 , 來制定以條約為基礎的機構 , 來填補那些治理空間 , 那麼剩下的弱點會怎麼樣 ?
and that's a big problem , and we'll return to it in just a second .	這是個大問題 , 我們只要一秒鐘就回來 。
so there's my first message , that if you are to pass through these turbulent times more or less turbulently , then our success in doing that will in large measure depend on our capacity to bring sensible governance to the global space .	所以 , 我的第一個訊息是 , 如果你要通過這些亂流 , 或多或少的亂流 , 那麼 , 我們的成功將會取決於我們的能力 , 將可感應的治理帶給全球空間 。
and watch that beginning to happen .	看看這個開始發生的 。
my second point is , and i know i don't have to talk to an audience like this about such a thing , but power is not just shifting vertically , it's also shifting horizontally .	我的第二個重點是 , 我知道我不用跟這樣的觀眾說話 , 像這樣的話 , 但權力不僅是垂直轉換 , 它也在橫向轉移 。
you might argue that the story , the history of civilizations , has been civilizations gathered around seas with the first ones around the mediterranean , the more recent ones in the ascendents of western power around the atlantic .	你可能會說 , 文明的歷史早已在海邊聚集了文明 , 最早在地中海附近的生物 , 在大西洋附近的西方國家 。
well it seems to me that we're now seeing a fundamental shift of power , broadly speaking , away from nations gathered around the atlantic [seaboard] to the nations gathered around the pacific rim .	對我來說 , 我們現在正看到一個基本的權力轉移 , 廣泛地說話 , 遠離大西洋岸的國家 , 聚集到太平洋岸附近的國家 。
now that begins with economic power , but that's the way it always begins .	經濟力量始於此 , 但這一直是這樣開始的 。
you already begin to see the development of foreign policies , the augmentation of military budgets occurring in the other growing powers in the world .	你已經開始看到外交政策的發展 , 軍事預算的擴增發生在世界上其他種植的力量 。
i think actually this is not so much a shift from the west to the east ; something different is happening .	我認為這並不是從西方轉移到東方 , 不一樣的事情正在發生 。
my guess is , for what it's worth , is that the united states will remain the most powerful nation on earth for the next 10 years , 15 , but the context in which she holds her power has now radically altered ; it has radically changed .	我的猜測是 , 值得的 , 是美國在接下來的十年 , 將維持在地球上最強大的國家 , 15年 , 但她握有權力的背景已經徹底改變 ; 它徹底地改變了 。
we are coming out of 50 years , most unusual years , of history in which we have had a totally monopolar world , in which every compass needle for or against has to be referenced by its position to washington a world bestrode by a single colossus .	我們從五十年來 , 最不尋常的歷史 , 我們有完全單一的世界 , 每一根針或對它的位置都需要被華盛頓世界最好的地位來參考 。
but that's not a usual case in history .	但這不是歷史上常見的例子 。
in fact , what's now emerging is the much more normal case of history .	事實上 , 現在出現的是更正常的歷史案例 。
you're beginning to see the emergence of a multipolar world .	你開始看到一個多重世界的出現 。
up until now , the united states has been the dominant feature of our world .	目前為止 , 美國一直是世界主要的特徵 。
they will remain the most powerful nation , but they will be the most powerful nation in an increasingly multipolar world .	他們會維持最強大的國家 , 但他們會是越來越多世界中最強大的國家 。
and you begin to see the alternative centers of power building up in china , of course , though my own guess is that china's ascent to greatness is not smooth .	當然 , 你開始看到在中國建立的其他權力中心 , 但我自己的猜測是 , 中國的權力不是光滑的 。
it's going to be quite grumpy as china begins to democratize her society after liberalizing her economy .	中國將開始在自由化經濟後讓她的社會變得很糟糕 。
but that's a subject of a different discussion .	但這是個不同的討論題目 。
you see india , you see brazil .	你看印度 , 巴西 。
you see increasingly that the world now looks actually , for us europeans , much more like europe in the 19th century .	你可以看到 , 越來越多的歐洲人在19世紀看起來更像歐洲 。
europe in the 19th century: a great british foreign secretary , lord canning , used to describe it as the " european concert of powers . "	歐洲在十九世紀 , 一個偉大的英國外國秘書長候選人 , 曾經把它描述為 「 歐洲的權力協會 」 。
there was a balance , a fivesided balance .	有一個平衡 , 一個五方的平衡 。
britain always played to the balance .	英國總是在平衡上演 。
if paris got together with berlin , britain got together with vienna and rome to provide a counterbalance .	如果巴黎和柏林團結起來 , 英國和維也納和羅馬合作 , 提供平衡 。
now notice , in a period which is dominated by a monopolar world , you have fixed alliances nato , the warsaw pact .	請注意 , 在一個由單一世界主宰的時代 , 你有固定的聯盟納托 , 戰神 。
a fixed polarity of power means fixed alliances .	一個固定的權力的兩極性意味著修正聯盟 。
but a multiple polarity of power means shifting and changing alliances .	但有多個兩極的權力 , 意味著改變和改變盟友 。
and that's the world we're coming into , in which we will increasingly see that our alliances are not fixed .	這就是我們要進入的世界 , 我們會漸漸看到我們的聯盟沒有固定 。
canning , the great british foreign secretary once said , " britain has a common interest , but no common allies . "	大英國外國秘書長曾說: 「 英國有一個共同的利益 , 但沒有共通盟友 。 」
and we will see increasingly that even we in the west will reach out , have to reach out , beyond the cozy circle of the atlantic powers to make alliances with others if we want to get things done in the world .	我們會越來越看到 , 即使我們在西方世界也能伸出援手 , 得要伸出援手 , 超越大西洋力量圈的瘋狂循環 , 來和他人聯盟 , 如果我們想要把事情做好 。
note , that when we went into libya , it was not good enough for the west to do it alone ; we had to bring others in .	注意到 , 當我們進入利比亞時 , 西方人不夠好 , 我們必須把他人帶進來 。
we had to bring , in this case , the arab league in .	我們必須帶入阿拉伯聯盟 。
my guess is iraq and afghanistan are the last times when the west has tried to do it themselves , and we haven't succeeded .	我猜伊拉克和阿富汗是最後一次 , 當西方嘗試自己做這件事時 , 我們還沒有成功 。
my guess is that we're reaching the beginning of the end of 400 years i say 400 years because it's the end of the ottoman empire of the hegemony of western power , western institutions and western values .	我的猜測是 , 我們已經達到400年的初期 , 我說400年了 , 因為這是西方權力的開端 , 西方體制和西方價值觀 。
you know , up until now , if the west got its act together , it could propose and dispose in every corner of the world .	你知道 , 一直到現在 , 如果西方人一起行動 , 它可以在世界各個角落提出和散播 。
but that's no longer true .	但這不再是事實了 。
take the last financial crisis after the second world war .	以第二次世界大戰後的金融危機為例 。
the west got together the bretton woods institution , world bank , international monetary fund the problem solved .	西方世界銀行 , 國際貨幣基金會解決了問題 。
now we have to call in others .	現在我們必須打電話給其他人 。
now we have to create the g20 .	現在我們必須創造g20 。
now we have to reach beyond the cozy circle of our western friends .	現在我們必須超越我們西方朋友的瘋狂圈 。
let me make a prediction for you , which is probably even more startling .	讓我為你們做個預測 , 這可能更令人驚訝 。
i suspect we are now reaching the end of 400 years when western power was enough .	我猜現在已經達到400年了 , 當時西方的權力已經夠了 。
people say to me , " the chinese , of course , they'll never get themselves involved in peacemaking , multilateral peacemaking around the world . "	人們對我說: 「 中國 , 當然 , 他們永遠不會讓自己參與世界各地的和平 。 」
oh yes ? why not ?	噢 ? 為什麼不 ?
how many chinese troops are serving under the blue beret , serving under the blue flag , serving under the u . n . command in the world today ?	有多少中國軍隊在藍色的防線下服務 , 在藍色的旗幟下服務 , 在聯合國的指令下服務 ?
how many americans ? 11 .	有多少美國人 ? 十一歲 。
what is the largest naval contingent tackling the issue of somali pirates ?	什麼是最大的海軍同意處理索馬利海盜的問題 ?
the chinese naval contingent .	中國的海軍集團 。
of course they are , they are a mercantilist nation .	當然 , 牠們是非種族主義的國家 。
they want to keep the sea lanes open .	他們想要讓海平線開放 。
increasingly , we are going to have to do business with people with whom we do not share values , but with whom , for the moment , we share common interests .	越來越多時候 , 我們得要和那些我們沒有共享價值的人做生意 , 但當下 , 我們分享共同利益 。
it's a whole new different way of looking at the world that is now emerging .	這是一個全新的角度來看世界 , 現在正在興起 。
and here's the third factor , which is totally different .	第三個因素 , 完全不同 。
today in our modern world , because of the internet , because of the kinds of things people have been talking about here , everything is connected to everything .	現今 , 在我們的現代世界 , 由於網路 , 人們一直在談論的事物 , 一切都與所有事物連結在一起 。
we are now interdependent .	我們現在是互相依賴的 。
we are now interlocked , as nations , as individuals , in a way which has never been the case before , never been the case before .	身為一個個體 , 我們現在是互相連結的 , 一個從來沒有發生過的案例 , 從來沒有發生過 。
the interrelationship of nations , well it's always existed .	國家之間的關聯 , 總是存在著 。
diplomacy is about managing the interrelationship of nations .	外交是要管理國家之間的關聯 。
but now we are intimately locked together .	但現在我們被關起來了 。
you get swine flu in mexico , it's a problem for charles de gaulle airport 24 hours later .	在墨西哥 , 查爾斯德高爾機場24小時後 , 你就會得到豬流感 。
lehman brothers goes down , the whole lot collapses .	雷曼兄弟會下降 , 全部都崩潰了 。
there are fires in the steppes of russia , food riots in africa .	俄羅斯有火災 , 非洲的食物暴動 。
we are all now deeply , deeply , deeply interconnected .	我們現在非常、非常、非常緊密連結 。
and what that means is the idea of a nation state acting alone , not connected with others , not working with others , is no longer a viable proposition .	這意味著 , 一個國家單獨行動的概念 , 不是與他人聯繫 , 而不是與他人合作 , 不再是一個可行的提議 。
because the actions of a nation state are neither confined to itself , nor is it sufficient for the nation state itself to control its own territory , because the effects outside the nation state are now beginning to affect what happens inside them .	因為一個國家的行動 , 既不被限制 , 也不足以控制國家本身的領土 , 因為外國的影響已經開始影響他們內在的狀況 。
i was a young soldier in the last of the small empire wars of britain .	我是英國最後一個小帝國戰爭的年輕士兵 。
at that time , the defense of my country was about one thing and one thing only: how strong was our army , how strong was our air force , how strong was our navy and how strong were our allies .	那時 , 我國家的防禦是一件事 , 只有一件事:我們的軍隊有多強壯 , 我們的空軍有多強壯 , 我們的海軍和我們的盟友有多強 。
that was when the enemy was outside the walls .	那時候敵人就在牆外 。
now the enemy is inside the walls .	敵人就在牆壁裡 。
now if i want to talk about the defense of my country , i have to speak to the minister of health because pandemic disease is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of agriculture because food security is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of industry because the fragility of our hitech infrastructure is now a point of attack for our enemies as we see from cyber warfare i have to speak to the minister of home affairs because who has entered my country , who lives in that terraced house in that inner city has a direct effect on what happens in my country as we in london saw in the 7/7 bombings .	如果我想要談我的國家國防部長 , 我必須和衛生部長談談 , 因為流行病對我的安全有威脅 , 我必須和農業部長談談 , 因為食物安全對我的國家是有威脅的 , 我必須和工業部談談 , 因為我們希臘基礎設施的脆弱 , 正是我們的敵人 , 我們從網路戰爭中看到的 , 我必須和國內部長談談 , 因為在國內 , 我們在這個城市中 , 正受到威脅 。
it's no longer the case that the security of a country is simply a matter for its soldiers and its ministry of defense .	不再是國家的安全對軍人和國防的重要性 。
it's its capacity to lock together its institutions .	它的能力可以把它的機構鎖起來 。
and this tells you something very important .	這告訴我們一件非常重要的事 。
it tells you that , in fact , our governments , vertically constructed , constructed on the economic model of the industrial revolution vertical hierarchy , specialization of tasks , command structures have got the wrong structures completely .	它告訴你 , 事實上 , 我們的政府 , 垂直建構 , 建立在工業革命的經濟模式上 , 垂直層級、專業化、指令結構完全有錯誤的結構 。
you in business know that the paradigm structure of our time , ladies and gentlemen , is the network .	你們知道我們這個時代的典範結構 , 各位先生女士 , 就是網路 。
it's your capacity to network that matters , both within your governments and externally .	這是你對網路很重要的能力 , 無論是在你的政府或外部 。
so here is ashdown's third law .	這裡是shown的第三個定律 。
by the way , don't ask me about ashdown's first law and second law because i haven't invented those yet ; it always sounds better if there's a third law , doesn't it ?	順道一提 , 不要問我關於阿什沃恩的第一條法律和第二定律 , 因為我還沒發明這些法律 ; 如果有第三條定律的話 , 聽起來比較好嗎 ?
ashdown's third law is that in the modern age , where everything is connected to everything , the most important thing about what you can do is what you can do with others .	shown的第三定律是 , 在現代 , 一切都和所有事情有關 , 最重要的是你能做的事 , 就是你能做些什麼 。
the most important bit about your structure whether you're a government , whether you're an army regiment , whether you're a business is your docking points , your interconnectors , your capacity to network with others .	關於你的結構 , 不論你是政府 , 不論你是軍隊註冊 , 不論你是企業 , 你的交叉點 , 你的交叉點 , 你和他人建立的能力 。
you understand that in industry ; governments don't .	在工業界 , 政府不了解 。
but now one final thing .	但 , 最後一件事 。
if it is the case , ladies and gentlemen and it is that we are now locked together in a way that has never been quite the same before , then it's also the case that we share a destiny with each other .	如果是這樣的情況 , 各位先生女士們 , 我們現在被關起來 , 以以前從來沒有完全相同的方式 , 那也是我們彼此之間的命運 。
suddenly and for the very first time , collective defense , the thing that has dominated us as the concept of securing our nations , is no longer enough .	突然間 , 第一次 , 集體防禦 , 佔據我們國家的概念 , 不再是足夠的 。
it used to be the case that if my tribe was more powerful than their tribe , i was safe ; if my country was more powerful than their country , i was safe ; my alliance , like nato , was more powerful than their alliance , i was safe .	以前 , 如果我的部落比他們的部落更強大 , 我很安全 ; 如果我的國家比他們的更強大 , 我更安全 ; 我的聯盟 , 像是納多 , 比他們的盟友更強大 , 我就安全了 。
it is no longer the case .	它不再是案例 。
the advent of the interconnectedness and of the weapons of mass destruction means that , increasingly , i share a destiny with my enemy .	相互關聯性和大規模毀滅的武器 , 意味著越來越多 , 我和敵人有了命運 。
when i was a diplomat negotiating the disarmament treaties with the soviet union in geneva in the 1970s , we succeeded because we understood we shared a destiny with them .	當我還是外交官時 , 和1970年代日內瓦的蘇聯和蘇聯的蘇聯談判 , 我們成功了 , 因為我們知道我們和他們共享一個命運 。
collective security is not enough .	集體安全還不夠 。
peace has come to northern ireland because both sides realized that the zerosum game couldn't work .	和平已經來到北愛爾蘭 , 因為兩者都意識到零和遊戲無法運作 。
they shared a destiny with their enemies .	他們和敵人共享命運 。
one of the great barriers to peace in the middle east is that both sides , both israel and , i think , the palestinians , do not understand that they share a collective destiny .	中東和平的一個大障礙 , 就是雙方 , 以色列 , 我認為 , 巴勒斯坦人 , 並不知道他們有共同的命運 。
and so suddenly , ladies and gentlemen , what has been the proposition of visionaries and poets down the ages becomes something we have to take seriously as a matter of public policy .	所以 , 各位先生女士們 , 先生們提議視覺和詩人在這個時代變成了我們必須認真看待的公共政策 。
i started with a poem , i'll end with one .	我從一首詩開始 , 用一首詩結束 。
the great poem of john donne's .	約翰•唐納的偉大詩 。
" send not for whom the bell tolls . "	「 不要把鈴聲送給誰 。 」
the poem is called " no man is an island . "	這首詩叫做 「 沒有人是孤島 。 」
and it goes: " every man's death affected me , for i am involved in mankind , send not to ask for whom the bell tolls , it tolls for thee . "	它說: 「 每個人的死亡都會影響到我 , 因爲我參與人類 , 不去問誰鈴聲 , 它會幫我取帳 。 」
for john donne , a recommendation of morality .	約翰.唐納的建議是道德的建議 。
for us , i think , part of the equation for our survival .	我認為 , 對我們生存的公式有一部分 。
to find the path to long life and health , dan buettner and team study the world's " blue zones , " communities whose elders live with vim and vigor to recordsetting age . at tedxtc , he shares the 9 common diet and lifestyle habits that keep them spry past age 100 .	為了尋找長壽和健康的路 , danbuettner和團隊研究世界的 「 藍色區域 」 , 他們的長者與vim和vigor一起生活 , 在tedxc分享了9個常見的飲食習慣 , 讓它們過去一百歲 。
biology , culture , exploration , food , health , life , science	生物學、文化、探索、食物、健康、生命、科學、科學、科學、科學、科學、科學、科學、科學、科學、科學、科學、科學、
dan buettner: how to live to be 100+	danbuettner:如何活到100+100 。
something called the danish twin study established that only about 10 percent of how long the average person lives , within certain biological limits , is dictated by our genes .	丹麥雙胞胎研究發現 , 一般人的壽命只有百分之十 , 在某些生物限制下 , 由我們的基因決定 。
the other 90 percent is dictated by our lifestyle .	剩下的90%是由我們的生活方式決定 。
so the premise of blue zones: if we can find the optimal lifestyle of longevity we can come up with a de facto formula for longevity .	所以 , 藍色區域的前提是:如果我們能找到長壽的最佳生活方式 , 我們就能找到一個對長壽的事實公式 。
but if you ask the average american what the optimal formula of longevity is , they probably couldn't tell you .	但如果你問一般的美國人 , 長壽的最佳公式是什麼 , 他們可能不會告訴你 。
they've probably heard of the south beach diet , or the atkins diet .	他們可能聽過南海灘飲食 , 或皮膚飲食 。
you have the usda food pyramid .	你有美國食品金字塔 。
there is what oprah tells us .	歐普拉告訴我們 。
there is what doctor oz tells us .	奧茲博士告訴我們什麼 。
the fact of the matter is there is a lot of confusion around what really helps us live longer better .	事實是 , 對於真正幫助我們活得更久 , 有很多困惑 。
should you be running marathons or doing yoga ?	你該跑馬拉松還是瑜伽 ?
should you eat organic meats or should you be eating tofu ?	你該吃有機肉還是吃豆腐 ?
when it comes to supplements , should you be taking them ?	談到補充品 , 你該把它們帶走嗎 ?
how about these hormones or resveratrol ?	這些賀爾蒙或反轉戲院呢 ?
and does purpose play into it ?	目的是否會對它產生影響 ?
spirituality ? and how about how we socialize ?	靈性 ? 以及我們如何社會化 ?
well , our approach to finding longevity was to team up with national geographic , and the national institute on aging , to find the four demographically confirmed areas that are geographically defined .	我們尋找長壽的方法是與國家地理研究所合作 , 以及國家老化研究所合作 , 找出四個人口確認地理位置 。
and then bring a team of experts in there to methodically go through exactly what these people do , to distill down the crosscultural distillation .	再把專家團隊帶到那裡 , 來處理這些人的做法 , 來分辨跨文化的分裂 。
and at the end of this i'm going to tell you what that distillation is .	最後我要告訴各位 , 那個區分是什麼 。
but first i'd like to debunk some common myths when it comes to longevity .	但首先 , 我想破壞一些常見的迷思 , 談到長壽 。
and the first myth is if you try really hard you can live to be 100 .	第一個迷思是 , 如果你真的很難活到100歲 。
the problem is , only about one out of 5 , 000 people in america live to be 100 .	問題是 , 美國五千人當中只有一人活到一百歲 。
your chances are very low .	你的可能性非常低 。
even though it's the fastest growing demographic in america , it's hard to reach 100 .	儘管它是美國成長最快的人口 , 很難達到100歲 。
the problem is that we're not programmed for longevity .	問題是 , 我們沒有長壽編寫 。
we are programmed for something called procreative success .	我們被設計為 「 促進式成功 」 。
i love that word .	我很喜歡那個字 。
it reminds me of my college days .	它讓我想起我的大學日 。
biologists term procreative success to mean the age where you have children and then another generation , the age when your children have children .	生物學家稱作 「 優秀的成功 」 , 代表有孩子的年齡 , 接著是另一個世代 , 當你的孩子有孩子的年齡 。
after that the effect of evolution completely dissipates .	演化的影響完全消失了 。
if you're a mammal , if you're a rat or an elephant , or a human , in between , it's the same story .	如果你是哺乳動物 , 如果你是老鼠或大象 , 或人類 , 在兩者之間 , 則是同一個故事 。
so to make it to age 100 , you not only have to have had a very good lifestyle , you also have to have won the genetic lottery .	所以 , 要把它變成一百歲 , 你不只需要有很好的生活方式 , 你還得要贏得基因彩票 。
the second myth is , there are treatments that can help slow , reverse , or even stop aging .	第二個迷思是 , 有治療可以幫助緩慢、反轉 , 甚至阻止老化 。
when you think of it , there is 99 things that can age us .	想想看 , 有99件事情可以讓我們變老 。
deprive your brain of oxygen for just a few minutes , those brain cells die , they never come back .	剝奪氧氣的大腦幾分鐘 , 這些腦細胞會死亡 , 它們永遠不會回來 。
play tennis too hard , on your knees , ruin your cartilage , the cartilage never comes back .	彈網球太硬 , 在你的膝蓋上 , 破壞你的軟骨 , 軟骨永遠不會回來 。
our arteries can clog . our brains can gunk up with plaque , and we can get alzheimer's .	我們的動脈可以堵塞 。 我們的大腦可以用普拉克槍枝 , 我們可以得到阿茲海默症 。
there is just too many things to go wrong .	有太多事要出錯 。
our bodies have 35 trillion cells , trillion with a " t . " we're talking national debt numbers here .	我們的身體有35兆個細胞 , 有t 。 我們正在說國家債務數字 。
those cells turn themselves over once every eight years .	這些細胞每八年就會自轉一次 。
and every time they turn themselves over there is some damage . and that damage builds up .	每當他們轉身到那裡時 , 就會造成傷害 。
and it builds up exponentially .	它是指數型的 。
it's a little bit like the days when we all had beatles albums or eagles albums and we'd make a copy of that on a cassette tape , and let our friends copy that cassette tape , and pretty soon , with successive generations that tape sounds like garbage .	有點像是當我們有披頭四或老鷹專輯時 , 我們會在錄音帶上做複製 , 讓朋友複製錄音帶 , 很快地 , 帶有成功的世代聽起來像是垃圾 。
well , the same things happen to our cells .	同樣的事也會發生在我們的細胞身上 。
that's why a 65yearold person is aging at a rate of about 125 times faster than a 12yearold person .	這就是為什麼一個65歲的人老化速度比12歲的人快125倍 。
so , if there is nothing you can do to slow your aging or stop your aging , what am i doing here ?	所以 , 如果沒有任何事可以減緩老化或阻止老化 , 我在這裡做什麼 ?
well , the fact of the matter is the best science tells us that the capacity of the human body , my body , your body , is about 90 years , a little bit more for women .	問題是 , 最好的科學告訴我們人類身體的能力 , 我的身體 , 你的身體大約是90年 , 對於女性來說 , 多一點點 。
but life expectancy in this country is only 78 .	但這個國家的平均壽命只有78 。
so somewhere along the line , we're leaving about 12 good years on the table .	所以 , 在這條線的某處 , 我們留下了大約12年的好處 。
these are years that we could get .	這些年是我們可以得到的 。
and research shows that they would be years largely free of chronic disease , heart disease , cancer and diabetes .	研究顯示 , 牠們會多年免於慢性疾病、心臟疾病、癌症和糖尿病 。
we think the best way to get these missing years is to look at the cultures around the world that are actually experiencing them , areas where people are living to age 100 at rates up to 10 times greater than we are , areas where the life expectancy is an extra dozen years , the rate of middle age mortality is a fraction of what it is in this country .	我們認為最好的辦法是看看世界上的文化 , 人們生活在一百歲以上比我們高十倍的地方 , 平均壽命是十多年 , 中年死亡率的比例是這個國家的一小部分 。
we found our first blue zone about 125 miles off the coast of italy , on the island of sardinia .	我們在義大利海岸發現了第一塊藍色區域 , 大約離義大利的125英哩 , 在斯坦尼亞島 。
and not the entire island , the island is about 1 . 4 million people , but only up in the highlands , an area called the nuoro province .	不是整個島嶼 , 島嶼大約有140萬人 , 但只有在高地 , 一個叫做努羅省的區域 。
and here we have this area where men live the longest , about 10 times more centenarians than we have here in america .	這裡有一塊區域 , 男性壽命最長的百歲人 , 比美國多出十倍 。
and this is a place where people not only reach age 100 , they do so with extraordinary vigor .	這個地方 , 人們不僅達到一百歲 , 還帶著非凡的惡魔 。
places where 102 year olds still ride their bike to work , chop wood , and can beat a guy 60 years younger than them .	102歲的老人仍然騎腳踏車去上班 , 可比他們年輕60歲 。
their history actually goes back to about the time of christ .	他們的歷史回到了克里斯特的時代 。
it's actually a bronze age culture that's been isolated .	它其實是被孤立的青銅文化 。
because the land is so infertile , they largely are shepherds , which occasions regular , lowintensity physical activity .	因為土地很生育 , 大多是牧羊人 , 偶爾會規律、低密度的身體活動 。
their diet is mostly plantbased , accentuated with foods that they can carry into the fields .	他們的飲食大部分是以植物為基礎的 , 主要是以食物為主 , 他們可以帶到田裡 。
they came up with an unleavened whole wheat bread called carta musica made out of durum wheat , a type of cheese made from grassfed animals so the cheese is high in omega3 fatty acids instead of omega6 fatty acids from cornfed animals , and a type of wine that has three times the level of polyphenols than any known wine in the world .	他們想出了一片無盡的麥麵包 , 叫做卡塔音樂 , 由杜魯米麥所製成 , 一種乳酪 , 由於草草原的動物製造 , 所以乳酪在omega-3脂肪酸而不是omega-6脂肪酸 , 而是來自玉米飼料的動物 , 還有一種葡萄酒的類型 , 比世界上任何已知的葡萄酒都多三倍 。
but the real secret i think lies more in the way that they organize their society .	但我認為真正的秘密是他們組織社會的方式 。
and one of the most salient elements of the sardinian society is how they treat older people .	薩丁尼亞社會中最重要的元素之一就是他們如何對待老人的方式 。
you ever notice here in america , social equity seems to peak at about age 24 ?	你有沒有注意到在美國 , 社會平等似乎在24歲時達到高峰 ?
just look at the advertisements .	看看廣告 。
here in sardinia , the older you get the more equity you have , the more wisdom you're celebrated for .	在斯坦尼亞 , 你得到越多的平等 , 你所慶祝的智慧越多 。
you go into the bars in sardinia , instead of seeing the sports illustrated swimsuit calendar , you see the centenarian of the month calendar .	你走進薩丁尼亞的酒吧 , 而不是看到運動畫出游泳日曆 , 你會看到一個月的百歲人 。
this , as it turns out , is not only good for your aging parents to keep them close to the family it imparts about four to six years of extra life expectancy research shows it's also good for the children of those families , who have lower rates of mortality and lower rates of disease .	結果發現 , 這不只對你的老年父母保持親近家庭的好處 , 預期壽命短短短四到六年的研究顯示 , 對那些家庭的孩子來說 , 死亡率和疾病的比率較低 。
that's called the grandmother effect .	這叫做祖母效應 。
we found our second blue zone on the other side of the planet , about 800 miles south of tokyo , on the archipelago of okinawa .	我們在地球的另一邊找到了第二塊藍色區域 , 大約是東京的800英里南部 , 俄亥俄州的阿根比拉哥 。
okinawa is actually 161 small islands .	okinawa其實是161個小島 。
and in the northern part of the main island , this is ground zero for world longevity .	在主要島的北部 , 這是世上長壽的地點 。
this is a place where the oldest living female population is found .	這個地方是最古老的女性族群 。
it's a place where people have the longest disabilityfree life expectancy in the world .	這個地方 , 人們有世界上最長的殘疾壽命 。
they have what we want .	他們有我們想要的 。
they live a long time , and tend to die in their sleep , very quickly , and often , i can tell you , after sex .	牠們活得很久 , 牠們的睡眠很快 , 通常 , 我會告訴你 , 在性愛之後 , 我會告訴你 。
they live about seven good years longer than the average american .	他們比平均美國人活了七年 。
five times as many centenarians as we have in america .	美國有五倍的百歲人 。
one fifth the rate of colon and breast cancer , big killers here in america .	五分之一的殖民地癌症和乳癌 , 在美國是很大的殺手 。
and one sixth the rate of cardiovascular disease .	第六種心血管疾病的速率 。
and the fact that this culture has yielded these numbers suggests strongly they have something to teach us .	這種文化產生了這些數字 , 強而有力地指出 , 它們有可以教我們的東西 。
what do they do ?	他們會怎麼做 ?
once again , a plantbased diet , full of vegetables with lots of color in them .	再一次 , 以植物為基礎的飲食 , 滿是蔬菜 , 裡面有很多顏色 。
and they eat about eight times as much tofu as americans do .	他們吃的比美國人多了八倍 。
more significant than what they eat is how they eat it .	比牠們吃的東西更重要的是牠們如何吃它 。
they have all kinds of little strategies to keep from overeating , which , as you know , is a big problem here in america .	他們有各式各樣的小策略來阻止過度濫用 , 如你所知 , 這問題在美國是很大的問題 。
a few of the strategies we observed: they eat off of smaller plates , so they tend to eat fewer calories at every sitting .	我們觀察到的一些策略是:它們從小盤子中吃掉 , 所以它們通常會在每個坐下的卡路里減少 。
instead of serving family style , where you can sort of mindlessly eat as you're talking , they serve at the counter , put the food away , and then bring it to the table .	與其提供家庭風格 , 不如你在說話時 , 你可以輕鬆地吃飯 , 他們在櫃台上服務 , 把食物送到餐桌上 。
they also have a 3 , 000yearold adage , which i think is the greatest sort of diet suggestion ever invented .	他們還有一個3000歲的廣告 , 我認為這是史上最偉大的飲食建議 。
it was invented by confucius .	它是由混合體發明的 。
and that diet is known as the hara , hatchi , bu diet .	這種飲食被稱為 「 哈拉、哈特、佛飲食 」 。
it's simply a little saying these people say before their meal to remind them to stop eating when their stomach is [80] percent full .	簡單來說 , 這些人在吃飯之前就說過要提醒他們 , 不要再吃八成 。
it takes about a half hour for that full feeling to travel from your belly to your brain .	整個感覺需要半小時才能從腹部傳送到你的大腦 。
and by remembering to stop at 80 percent it helps keep you from doing that very thing .	記得80%的時間 , 它會讓你無法做這件事 。
but , like sardinia , okinawa has a few social constructs that we can associate with longevity .	但 , 像sardinia , okinawa有幾個社會結構 , 可以讓我們和長壽相關 。
we know that isolation kills .	我們知道孤立會致命 。
fifteen years ago , the average american had three good friends .	15年前 , 一般的美國人有三個好朋友 。
we're down to one and half right now .	我們現在已經降到一半了 。
if you were lucky enough to be born in okinawa , you were born into a system where you automatically have a half a dozen friends with whom you travel through life .	如果你幸運地出生在俄克inawa , 你就出生在一個系統中 , 自動地有五十個朋友 , 和你經歷過生命 。
they call it a moai . and if you're in a moai you're expected to share the bounty if you encounter luck , and if things go bad , child gets sick , parent dies , you always have somebody who has your back .	他們稱之為 「 摩艾 」 , 如果你在摩艾公司 , 你預期會分享 「 不好 」 , 如果你遇到運氣 , 如果事情不好 , 孩子生病 , 父母死亡 , 你總是會有人背負你 。
this particular moai , these five ladies have been together for 97 years .	這個獨特的摩艾 , 這五位女士已經聚集了97年 。
their average age is 102 .	平均年齡是102歲 。
typically in america we've divided our adult life up into two sections .	通常在美國 , 我們把成人的生命分成兩區 。
there is our work life , where we're productive .	我們的工作是有生產力的 。
and then one day , boom , we retire .	有一天 , 我們退休了 。
and typically that has meant retiring to the easy chair , or going down to arizona to play golf .	一般來說 , 這意味著退休到簡單的椅子上 , 或是去亞利桑那州打高爾夫球 。
in the okinawan language there is not even a word for retirement .	在俄克林納的語言中 , 甚至沒有退休的詞語 。
instead there is one word that imbues your entire life , and that word is " ikigai . "	相反地 , 有一種詞會傳染你的一生 , 那個字就是 「 ikigai 」 。
and , roughly translated , it means " the reason for which you wake up in the morning . "	大概翻譯了一下 , 意思是: 「 你早上醒來的理由 。 」
for this 102yearold karate master , his ikigai was carrying forth this martial art .	這位102歲的karate碩士 , 他的ikigai正在執行這場戰術 。
for this hundredyearold fisherman it was continuing to catch fish for his family three times a week .	對於這個百歲的漁民來說 , 每週捕魚三次 。
and this is a question . the national institute on aging actually gave us a questionnaire to give these centenarians .	這是個問題 。 國家老化研究所給了我們一個問卷 , 來給這些百歲人 。
and one of the questions , they were very culturally astute , the people who put the questionnaire .	其中一個問題是 , 他們是非常文化的研究者 , 把問題問卷的人 。
one of the questions was , " what is your ikigai ? "	其中一個問題是: 「 你的ikigai是什麼 ? 」
they instantly knew why they woke up in the morning .	他們馬上就知道為什麼早上起床 。
for this 102 year old woman , her ikigai was simply her greatgreatgreatgranddaughter .	對於這位102歲的女子來說 , 她的伊基加伊只是她的曾曾曾曾孫女 。
two girls separated in age by 101 and a half years .	兩個女孩在101年分離 。
and i asked her what it felt like to hold a greatgreatgreatgranddaughter .	我問她 , 拿著一位曾曾曾祖父的感覺是什麼樣的感覺 。
and she put her head back and she said , " it feels like leaping into heaven . "	她回頭說: 「 感覺就像跳進天堂 。 」
i thought that was a wonderful thought .	我覺得那是個很棒的想法 。
my editor at geographic wanted me to find america's blue zone .	我在地理位置的編輯希望我能找到美國的藍色區域 。
and for a while we looked on the prairies of minnesota , where actually there is a very high proportion of centenarians .	一陣子我們看了明尼蘇達的草原 , 實際上 , 百歲人的比例非常高 。
but that's because all the young people left .	但那是因為所有的年輕人都離開了 。
so , we turned to the data again .	所以 , 我們又轉向資料 。
and we found america's longestlived population among the seventhday adventists concentrated in and around loma linda , california .	我們發現美國最長壽的人口 , 是在加州洛馬林達州的第七天冒險家中 。
adventists are conservative methodists .	激進分子是保守的方法主義者 。
they celebrate their sabbath from sunset on friday till sunset on saturday .	他們在星期五日的日落慶祝他們的安息日 , 直到星期六 。
a " 24hour sanctuary in time , " they call it .	他們稱之為 「 時代24小時的庇護所 」
and they follow five little habits that conveys to them extraordinary longevity , comparatively speaking .	他們遵循五個小習慣 , 傳遞給他們非凡的長壽 。
in america here , life expectancy for the average woman is 80 .	在美國 , 平均女性的平均壽命是80歲 。
but for an adventist woman , their life expectancy is 89 .	但對於一個先進的女人來說 , 他們的預期壽命是89歲 。
and the difference is even more pronounced among men , who are expected to live about 11 years longer than their american counterparts .	男性之間的差別更為明顯 , 他們預期的比美國人活了11年 。
now , this is a study that followed about 70 , 000 people for 30 years .	這個研究追蹤了約七萬人三十年 。
sterling study . and i think it supremely illustrates the premise of this blue zone project .	史特林研究 , 我認為它總會說明這個藍色區域計畫的前提 。
this is a heterogeneous community .	這是一個異質的社區 。
it's white , black , hispanic , asian .	是白人、黑人、西班牙人、亞洲人 。
the only thing that they have in common are a set of very small lifestyle habits that they follow ritualistically for most of their lives .	他們唯一的共通點是一套非常小型的生活習慣 , 他們大部分的時間都遵循著儀式 。
they take their diet directly from the bible .	他們直接從聖經中獲得飲食 。
genesis: chapter one , verse [29] , where god talks about legumes and seeds , and on one more stanza about green plants , ostensibly missing is meat .	金恩斯:第一章 , 正是29 。 上帝談到法律和種子 , 在另一個斯坦扎亞 , 關於綠色植物 , 很明顯缺失的就是肉 。
they take this sanctuary in time very serious .	他們非常認真地認真看待這個庇護時期 。
for 24 hours every week , no matter how busy they are , how stressed out they are at work , where the kids need to be driven , they stop everything and they focus on their god , their social network , and then , hardwired right in the religion , are nature walks .	每週24小時 , 不論他們多忙、工作有多緊張 , 孩子們需要被驅使、阻止一切 , 他們把焦點放在上帝、社交網路 , 然後就在宗教中 , 天性會走路 。
and the power of this is not that it's done occasionally , the power is it's done every week for a lifetime .	這種力量並不偶爾會產生 , 它的力量是每週都在完成的 。
none of it's hard . none of it costs money .	沒有一個是困難的 。 沒有一個花錢 。
adventists also tend to hang out with other adventists .	基督徒也傾向於與其他先進分子混在一起 。
so , if you go to an adventist's party you don't see people swilling jim beam or rolling a joint .	所以 , 如果你去參加一個冒險派對 , 你看不到人們在揮舞吉姆貝姆或轉動關節 。
instead they're talking about their next nature walk , exchanging recipes , and yes , they pray .	相反地 , 他們談的是下一天的走路 , 交換食譜 , 沒錯 , 他們祈禱 。
but they influence each other in profound and measurable ways .	但它們會以深刻且可測量的方式影響彼此 。
this is a culture that has yielded ellsworth whareham .	這個文化產生了 「 埃爾斯威爾漢 」 。
ellsworth whareham is 97 years old .	埃爾斯•威爾罕是97歲 。
he's a multimillionaire , yet when a contractor wanted 6 , 000 dollars to build a privacy fence , he said , " for that kind of money i'll do it myself . "	他是個數百萬富翁 , 但當一個包商想要六千美金來建造一個隱私的柵欄時 , 他說: 「 為了那類的錢 , 我會自己做 。 」
so for the next three days he was out shoveling cement , and hauling poles around .	所以 , 接下來的三天 , 他出去吃水泥 , 四處游去 。
and predictably , perhaps , on the fourth day he ended up in the operating room .	或許 , 在第四天 , 他最後進了手術室 。
but not as the guy on the table ; the guy doing openheart surgery .	但不是坐在桌上的人 , 而是開心手術的人 。
at 97 he still does 20 openheart surgeries every month .	97歲時 , 他每個月還會做二十次開心手術 。
ed rawlings , 103 years old now , an active cowboy , starts his morning with a swim .	艾德•羅林斯 , 103歲 , 一個活躍的牛仔 , 早上開始游泳 。
and on weekends he likes to put on the boards , throw up rooster tails .	在週末 , 他喜歡戴上板子 , 丟出rooster尾巴 。
her grandson actually lives in the twin cities here .	她的孫子其實住在雙胞胎城市 。
she starts her day with lifting weights .	她每天從舉重開始 。
she rides her bicycle .	她騎腳踏車 。
and then she gets in her rootbeer colored 1994 cadillac seville , and tears down the san bernardino freeway , where she still volunteers for seven different organizations .	然後她在她的根部裡彩色了1994年的卡迪拉克•塞維爾 , 戴著聖貝納多的高速公路 , 在那裡她仍然為七個不同的組織志工 。
i've been on 19 hardcore expeditions .	我曾經歷過19次硬幣探險 。
i'm probably the only person you'll ever meet who rode his bicycle across the sahara desert without sunscreen .	我可能是唯一一個穿過撒哈拉沙漠的自行車的人 。
but i'll tell you , there is no adventure more harrowing than riding shotgun with marge deton .	但我會告訴各位 , 冒險的程度遠遠遠比起和瑪奇•丹頓騎機更嚴厲 。
" a stranger is a friend i haven't met yet ! " she'd say to me .	「 陌生人是我還沒見過的朋友 ! 」 她會對我說 。
so , what are the common denominators in these three cultures ?	所以 , 這三種文化中有什麼共同點 ?
what are the things that they all do ?	他們會做些什麼 ?
and we managed to boil it down to nine .	我們成功地把它歸結為九個 。
in fact we've done two more blue zone expeditions since this and these common denominators hold true .	事實上 , 我們已經再做了兩次藍色區域探險 , 和這些共同點 , 都是真的 。
and the first one , and i'm about to utter a heresy here , none of them exercise , at least the way we think of exercise .	首先 , 我會在這裡進行一場演說 , 沒有一個運動 , 至少我們認為運動的方式 。
instead , they set up their lives so that they are constantly nudged into physical activity .	相反地 , 他們設立了自己的人生 , 以便他們不斷地被迫進入實體活動 。
these 100yearold okinawan women are getting up and down off the ground , they sit on the floor , 30 or 40 times a day .	這些百歲的okinawan女性在地面上上上下 , 她們每天坐著30到40次 。
sardinians live in vertical houses , up and down the stairs .	薩丁尼亞人住在垂直的房子裡 , 上下樓 。
every trip to the store , or to church or to a friend's house occasions a walk .	每次到商店 , 或教堂 , 或朋友的房子偶爾會走路 。
they don't have any conveniences .	他們沒有任何方便 。
there is not a button to push to do yard work or house work .	不需要按鈕來做院子或房子工作 。
if they want to mix up a cake , they're doing it by hand .	如果他們想混合蛋糕 , 他們會用手做 。
that burns calories just as much as going on the treadmill does .	跑步機的燃燒卡路里和跑步機一樣 。
when they do do intentional physical activity , it's the things they enjoy . they tend to walk , the only proven way to stave off cognitive decline , and they all tend to have a garden .	當他們做刻意的身體活動時 , 他們很享受 。 他們傾向於走路 , 唯一能證明認知衰退的方法 , 而且他們都傾向於有花園 。
they know how to set up their life in the right way so they have the right outlook .	他們知道如何以正確的方式建立生命 , 讓他們有正確的外觀 。
each of these cultures take time to downshift .	每種文化都需要時間降低 。
the sardinians pray . the seventhday adventists pray .	薩丁尼亞人祈禱 。 第七天的冒險家祈禱 。
the okinawans have this ancestor veneration .	okinawans有這種祖先的神經 。
but when you're in a hurry or stressed out , that triggers something called the inflammatory response , which is associated with everything from alzheimer's disease to cardiovascular disease .	但當你急著或緊張時 , 會觸發一種叫做發炎反應的東西 , 它會和阿茲海默症及心血管疾病有關 。
when you slow down for 15 minutes a day you turn that inflammatory state into a more antiinflammatory state .	當你每天放慢15分鐘 , 你就會把這種發炎狀態變成更加抗炎的狀態 。
they have vocabulary for sense of purpose , ikigai , like the okinawans .	他們有詞彙的意義 , 即ikigai , 像是okinawans 。
you know the two most dangerous years in your life are the year you're born , because of infant mortality , and the year you retire .	你知道你生命中最危險的兩年是你出生的那一年 , 因為嬰兒死亡率 , 而你退休的那一年 。
these people know their sense of purpose , and they activate in their life , that's worth about seven years of extra life expectancy .	這些人知道自己的目的 , 他們活躍了七年的預期壽命 。
there's no longevity diet .	沒有長壽的飲食 。
instead , these people drink a little bit every day , not a hard sell to the american population .	相反地 , 這些人每天都喝一點飲料 , 而不是很難賣給美國人口 。
they tend to eat a plantbased diet .	他們傾向會吃植物的飲食 。
doesn't mean they don't eat meat , but lots of beans and nuts .	不代表牠們不吃肉 , 而是大豆和堅果 。
and they have strategies to keep from overeating , little things that nudge them away from the table at the right time .	他們有策略 , 避免過度濫用 , 一些小事 , 讓它們在適當的時間離開桌子 。
and then the foundation of all this is how they connect .	這一切的基礎是它們如何連結 。
they put their families first , take care of their children and their aging parents .	他們先照顧他們的家人 , 照顧他們的孩子和老年父母 。
they all tend to belong to a faithbased community , which is worth between four and 14 extra years of life expectancy if you do it four times a month .	他們都歸屬於信仰型的社區 , 價值於四到十四年的預期壽命 , 如果你每個月做四次 。
and the biggest thing here is they also belong to the right tribe .	最重要的是 , 它們也屬於正確的部落 。
they were either born into or they proactively surrounded themselves with the right people .	他們不是出生就好 , 或主動地把自己和對的人聚在一起 。
we know from the framingham studies , that if your three best friends are obese there is a 50 percent better chance that you'll be overweight .	我們從弗林漢研究中得知 , 如果你的三個最好的朋友過胖了50%的機率會是過重的 。
so , if you hang out with unhealthy people , that's going to have a measurable impact over time .	所以 , 如果你和不健康的人混在一起 , 會隨著時間產生很大的影響 。
instead , if your friend's idea of recreation is physical activity , bowling , or playing hockey , biking or gardening , if your friends drink a little , but not too much , and they eat right , and they're engaged , and they're trusting and trustworthy , that is going to have the biggest impact over time .	取而代之 , 如果你的朋友對娛樂的看法是身體活動、弓 , 或玩曲棍球、腳踏車或園藝 , 如果你的朋友喝一點點 , 卻不太喜歡 , 他們會吃對了對的 , 而且他們很有信任和信任感 , 那會隨著時間產生最大的影響 。
diets don't work . no diet in the history of the world has ever worked for more than two percent of the population .	飲食不成功 , 世上沒有飲食 , 超過百分之二的人口 。
exercise programs usually start in january ; they're usually done by october .	運動計畫通常是一月開始的 ; 它們通常是十月完成的 。
when it comes to longevity there is no short term fix in a pill or anything else .	當談到長壽時 , 沒有短期的條件可以修復 , 或其他的條件 。
but when you think about it , your friends are longterm adventures , and therefore , perhaps the most significant thing you can do to add more years to your life , and life to your years . thank you very much .	但當你想一想時 , 你的朋友是長期冒險 , 因此 , 也許你能做的最重要的事 , 就是把更多年加上生命 , 感謝你 。
ink that conducts electricity ; a window that turns from clear to opaque at the flip of a switch ; a jelly that makes music . all this stuff exists , and catarina mota says: it's time to play with it . mota leads us on a tour of surprising and cool new materials , and suggests that the way we'll figure out what they're good for is to experiment , tinker and have fun .	墨水會產生電力 ; 一扇窗戶 , 從明確的轉向到不透明的開關 ; 水母會產生音樂 。 所有這些東西都存在 。 卡塔娜說:該是和它玩的時候了 。 莫塔將帶領我們驚訝又酷的新材料 , 並且建議我們找出它們的好處 , 做實驗、沉迷 , 並有樂趣 。
